	<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">Grade I listed buildings in West Yorkshire</h1>
	
	<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
		<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
		<div id="contentSub"></div>
		
		
		
		<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#p-search">Jump to search</a>

<p>There are over 9,000 <a href="/wiki/Grade_I_listed_building" class="mw-redirect" title="Grade I listed building">Grade I listed buildings</a> in <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">England</a>.  This page is a list of these buildings in the county of <a href="/wiki/West_Yorkshire" title="West Yorkshire">West Yorkshire</a>, by <a href="/wiki/Metropolitan_district" class="mw-redirect" title="Metropolitan district">metropolitan district</a>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes">Notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Grade_I_listed_buildings_in_West_Yorkshire&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="reflist" style="list-style-type: decimal;">
<div class="mw-references-wrap"><ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-EH_listed_building_header_note_1-1"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-EH_listed_building_header_note_1_1-0"><sup><i><b>a</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-EH_listed_building_header_note_1_1-1"><sup><i><b>b</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-EH_listed_building_header_note_1_1-2"><sup><i><b>c</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-EH_listed_building_header_note_1_1-3"><sup><i><b>d</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-EH_listed_building_header_note_1_1-4"><sup><i><b>e</b></i></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text">The date given is the date used by Historic England as significant for the initial building or that of an important part in the structure's description.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-EH_listed_building_header_note_2-2"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-EH_listed_building_header_note_2_2-0"><sup><i><b>a</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-EH_listed_building_header_note_2_2-1"><sup><i><b>b</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-EH_listed_building_header_note_2_2-2"><sup><i><b>c</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-EH_listed_building_header_note_2_2-3"><sup><i><b>d</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-EH_listed_building_header_note_2_2-4"><sup><i><b>e</b></i></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text">Sometimes known as OSGB36, the grid reference is based on the <a href="/wiki/British_national_grid_reference_system" class="mw-redirect" title="British national grid reference system">British national grid reference system</a> used by the <a href="/wiki/Ordnance_Survey" title="Ordnance Survey">Ordnance Survey</a>.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-EH_listed_building_header_note_3-3"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-EH_listed_building_header_note_3_3-0"><sup><i><b>a</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-EH_listed_building_header_note_3_3-1"><sup><i><b>b</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-EH_listed_building_header_note_3_3-2"><sup><i><b>c</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-EH_listed_building_header_note_3_3-3"><sup><i><b>d</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-EH_listed_building_header_note_3_3-4"><sup><i><b>e</b></i></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text">The "List Entry Number" is a unique number assigned to each listed building and scheduled monument by Historic England.</span>
</li>
</ol></div></div>
